 This astronomical event is Mercury transit ie Mercury transit
 9 may ko dopaher ko yekhagoleey ghatana shuru hogi
 Astronomical phenomena of Mercury transit can be seen across India
 pichhali baar ye khagoleey ghatana 2006 main hui thi
 What is Mercury transit? Mercury transit is an astronomical event in which the planet Mercury passes between the sun and the earth and all three celestial bodies are in a straight line
 aise main budh grah suraj ke gole par ek choti si kaali bindi kii tarah najar aata he
 The angular size of the planet Mercury is much less than that of the Sun, hence Mercury looks like a small black dot
 budh pargaman kii ghatana tab shuru hoti he jab budh grah kaa gola suraj ke gole ko choota hua najar aata he
 This is called the first touch of Mercury transit
 jaisehi budh grah kaa gola suraj kii chakri ke bheetar pahunch jaataa he
 This is called the second touch of Mercury transit
 iske baad budh grah kii kaali bindi suraj ke gole par aage badhati hui najar aati he
 When the sphere of the planet Mercury touches the sphere of the sun again from inside, it is called the third touch of Mercury transit
 jab budh grah kaa chota gola puri tarah se suraj ke gole ke paar ho jaataa he to ise chaturth sparsh yani chauthaa sparsh kehete hai or isi ke saath budh pargaman kii khagoleey ghatana khatm ho jaataa he
 The astronomical event of Mercury transit usually takes seven and a half hours
 budh pargaman main budh kaali bindi kii tarah kyon dikhataa he?ek shatabdi main 13-14 baar ghatit hotibudh grah suraj ke sabase paas kaa grah he
 It does not have its own light like the sun
 dharti or suraj ke bich main aane par budh kaa wo hissaa hamen dikhataa hajisapar suraj kii roshni nahin pad rahi hoti he
 Therefore, Mercury looks like black dot during transit on the bright sun
 budh pargaman ek durlabh aakashiya ghatana he
 It usually occurs 13 or 14 times in a century
 khaas baat ye he ki budh pargaman sirf or sirf may yaa november main hi hota he
 After transit in the month of November, Mercury transit takes place in the next November at an interval of 7, 13 or 33 years
 to vahiin may ke maheene main hua budh pargaman dobaaraa may ke maheene main 13 yaa 33 saal ke antaraal par hi hota he
 How to see Mercury transit? Mercury is only 158 parts of the shell of the spherical shell
 saath hi suraj kii chamak or garmi kisi ko bhi andhaa kar sakati he
 Because of this it is not easy to see Mercury transit
 budh pargaman dekhne main khaas saavdhaanee baraten nahin to aap andhe ho sakate hai
 Mercury transit can be seen by placing special solar filters on the telescope
 certyphoid solar filter or solar chashme lagaakar budh pargaman ko dekha ja saktaa he
 Do not try to look at the sun directly with the naked eye, this can cause your eyes to light up
 duniya bhar main budhpargaman kii drishyata9 may kaa budh pargaman asia ke zyaadaatar deshon (dakshin-purvi asia or japan ko chhodkar) main dekh jayega

 The seating arrangement or atmosphere at Cafe Coffee Day is also designed in such a way that people like to spend their time sitting here for hours and keep ordering something once in a while

 Bollywood rapper Badshah's new song "pagal" has set a new record on youtube
 badshaah ke gane pagal ko utyub par 24 ghante ke andar hi 7
 50 million views, which even Hollywood artist Taylor Swift has not been able to do till date
 isi ke saath badshaah ne korian boy band beaties ke april 2019 main banaae record ko tod diya he
 The funny thing is that despite breaking such a record and achieving great achievement, youtube has not given any congratulations or appreciation to youtube
 jabaki utyub ne apane plateform par sabase acha karne vaale gaanon kii saraahna kii thi
 These include songs by Ariana Grande, Thank You Next, Blackpink's Songs Kill This Love, bts's Boy With Love, and even Taylor Swift's Songs Me
 vaise is gane par record vyuj ko lekar do baaten chal rahi hai
 It is believed on Twitter that Badshah and his associates have bought views of crazy songs
 vahiin kuch kaa maananaa he ki badshaah ne google kii vigyapanon ko kharida he
 It is worth noting that many big artists buy advertisements to promote their songs
 aise main utyub par video ke bich main gane kii choti clip dikhaai jaati hai
 If viewers watch this clip for more than a few seconds, youtube counts it as one view
 ye vigyaapan kaa tarika tailor swift or blackpink ne bhi apanaaya he
 But it is believed that the emperor took it a little further
 badshaah kaa utyub par aaropis maamle main badshaah kaa kahana he ki utyub unke saath ninsaphi kar rahaa he
 youtube applauds the big international artists for their achievements, but is reluctant to mention the success of the Indian rapper
 bataa den ki badshaah bollywood ke bade raper hai
 He has sung and composed great and famous songs over the years
 badshaah kaa naam forbs kii 100 sabase amir bhartiya celibrities kii list main shaamil he

 film main sonakshi sinha mukhya kirdaar nibhaa rahi hai
 The film is releasing on August 2
 ajtak ke panchayat gujarat kaarykram ke ahm satr alpsankhyakon ke mudde main aasamaa khan pathan, sufi mehboob ali chishti, gayasuddin shaikh or noorjahan dewan ne shirkat kii
 The session was conducted by Punya Prasun Vajpayee
 pradhanmantri modi jab gujarat ke mukhyamantri the tab unhonesadbhaavna upwasakia tha
 Sufi Mehboob Ali Chishti was responsible for the participation of all religions in this fast
 ajtak ke manch par punya prasoon ne sufi mehboob ko yaad dilaayaa ki is upwas main modi ne topi pahanane se manaa kar diya tha
 Is this the model of Gujarat? is sawaal kaa jawaab dete hue sufi mehboob ali chishti ne kaha ki topi pahananaa or pehanaanaa desh kii raajnneeti nahin he
 Bringing Muslims into the mainstream of employment is an important issue
 gujarat bijepi alpsankhyak morcha ke pradesh adhyaksh sufi mehboob ali chishti ne kaha ki topi pahananaa or topi pehanaanaa hi kya vikaas he
 What hat did Gandhi to Sardar Patel ever wear
 haalanki isi vivaad par safai dete hue sufi chishti ne kaha ki moulana imam bukhari ko nimantran nahin diya gaya tha lekin jab vah vahaan pahunche to unhen manch par jagah de di gai
 He tried to do his politics through cap
 aasamaa khan pathan se sawaal poocha gaya ki kya gujarat main hinduon ke ilaake main or muslimon ko hinduon ke ilaake main rahane nahin diya jaataa
 On this Asma said that this is not only in Gujarat
 yahi chunauti maharashtra or karnataka main bhi dekhne ko milti he
 Asma said that the politics of appeasement was happening during the Congress era and this politics is the main reason for the backwardness of the Muslim society
 noorjahan dewan ne kaha ki hindu skulon main muslim bacchon ko daakhila nahin diya jaataa
 While recounting himself, Diwan said that he had to get his daughter enrolled in Hamdard School under compulsion
 haalanki manch se gayasuddin shaikh ne daawa kiya ki upie kaarykaal main alpsankhyak bacchon ko wajipha dene kaa elaan kiya tha lekin rajya main bijepi sarkaar ne teen saal tak us wajife ko jari nahin kiya
 This ignores the Modi government's slogan of Sabka Saath and Sabka Vikas
 ek sawaal ke jawaab main shaikh ne kaha ki gujarat main aajamusalmaan samudaay sabase zyada kamaikarta he
 But the credit for his earnings is not due to the BJP government in the state
 aisa mahaj isliye sambhav ho paaya he ki gujarat main hindu or musalmaan kandhaa se kandhaa milakar kaam karte hai or isi ke chalate unhen kamai ke achche maukey mili
 Sufi said that today there is a better environment in Gujarat, people are joining BJP
 muslim panchayat se lekar nagar palika ke chunaav main jitkar aa rahe he
 Gujarat is therefore riotous, crime free
 muslim samaaj bijepi se jud rahaa he, isiilie congress baichaiyn he
 He said that there have been riots every year during the Congress era
 gujarat ke siem bacchon ke admician ke liye muslim ke daravaaje par ja rahe hai
 Asma Pathan, director of the National Waqf Development Corporation, said that the Congress has done the work of planting poison among Hindu Muslims
 2002 ke baad gujarat main ajtak koi danga nahin hua he

 modi ji ne centre main aate hi alpsankhyak mantralay kaa fund badhaayaa

 musalamaanon kaa vikaas hindu bhai se zyada nahin chahie lekin baraabar kaa vikaas to chahie
 The court on Saturday reserved the verdict on the bail plea of juvenile, accused of killing seven-year-old Pradyuman Thakur, studying in second grade at Ryan International School in Gurugram
 jamaanat yachika par gurugram kii satr adaalat somvaar ko apana faisla sunayegi
 Earlier during the hearing on Thursday, the court sent the juvenile accused to a 14-day judicial custody at the child improvement home
 aaropee 16 varshiya chaatra reyaan international skool main hi 11veen main padhata he
 Pradyuman was brutally murdered on 8 September last year
 gurugram kishor nyaay board ne pichley varsh 20 disambar ko aadesh diya tha ki maamle main aaropee kishor par vayask maanakar mukadmaa chalaaya jayega

 vakil ne kaha ki varisht clinics manouvaigyanik dow

 No evidence was found against Ashoka
